    function getCommercialCookie(name) {
        var value = "; " + document.cookie;
        var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
        if (parts.length == 2) return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
        else return null;
    }
    function specialLayerEvent(specialLayer) {
        var links = document.getElementsByTagName('a');
        for(var i in links)
        {
            if(typeof links[i] !== 'object' || links[i] === null) {
                continue;
            }
            if(links[i].href.indexOf("javascript:void") > -1 || links[i].href.indexOf("#") > -1 || links[i].href.indexOf("prenumerata.rp.pl") > -1 || links[i].href.indexOf("archiwum.rp.pl") > -1 || links[i].href.indexOf(window.location.host+"/mapa") > -1 || links[i].href.indexOf("/rss") > -1 || links[i].href.indexOf("rankingi.rp.pl") > -1) {
                continue;
            }
            if((links[i].href.indexOf(".rp.pl") > -1 && links[i].href.indexOf(".rp.pl") < 30) || links[i].href.indexOf(".newscyclecloud.com") > -1 && links[i].href.indexOf(".newscyclecloud.com") < 30) {
                links[i].onclick = function(e){
                    e.preventDefault();
                    document.body.style.overflow = "hidden";
                    var targetHref = this.href;
                    history.pushState({}, '', Location.pathname);
                    window.onpopstate = function(event) {
                        if(event){
                            location.reload()
                        }
                    }
                    specialLayer.style.display = "block";
                    var midnight = new Date();
                    midnight.setHours(24,59,59,1);
                    document.cookie = "commercialBrake="+Date.now()+";expires="+midnight.toGMTString()+";path=/;domain="+window.location.hostname.match(/.\w*\.\w*$/gi)[0];
                    var countDownDate = new Date();
                    countDownDate.setTime(countDownDate.getTime() + 15500);
                    document.getElementsByClassName("special-layer-btn")[0].onclick = function(e){
                        window.location.href = targetHref;
                    }
                    var commercialTiemout = setInterval(function() {
                        var now = new Date().getTime();
                        var distance = countDownDate - now;
                        var seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);
                        switch (seconds) {
                        case 1:
                            document.getElementById("commercialBrakeSeconds").innerHTML = seconds + ' sekundę.';
                            break;
                        case 2:
                        case 3:
                        case 4:
                            document.getElementById("commercialBrakeSeconds").innerHTML = seconds + ' sekundy.';
                            break;
                        default:
                            document.getElementById("commercialBrakeSeconds").innerHTML = seconds + ' sekund.';
                        }
                        if (distance <= 14 || seconds <= 14) {
                            document.getElementsByClassName("special-layer-btn")[0].style.marginTop = '10px';
                        }
                        if (distance <= 0 || seconds <= 0) {
                            clearInterval(commercialTiemout);
                            window.location.href = targetHref;
                        }

                }
            }
        }

        function defaultOptions(options, defaults) {
            var result = defaults;
            for (var key in options) {
                if (options.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                    if (options[key] !== undefined) {
                        result[key] = options[key];
                    }

        }
        function scale(advertDOM, containerDOM, opt) {
            var scale      = containerDOM.offsetWidth / opt.width;
            var newLeftPos = Math.abs(Math.floor(((opt.width * scale) - opt.width)/2));
            var newTopPos  = Math.abs(Math.floor(((opt.height * scale) - opt.height)/2));
            var newHeight  = Math.abs(Math.floor(opt.height * scale));
            if (containerDOM.offsetWidth > opt.width) {
                return;
            }
            advertDOM.style.position   = 'relative';
            advertDOM.style.maxWidth   = 'none';
            advertDOM.style.width      = opt.width+'px';
            advertDOM.style.height     = opt.height+'px';
            advertDOM.style.transform  = 'scale('+scale+')';
            advertDOM.style.left       = '-'+newLeftPos+'px';
            advertDOM.style.top        = '-'+newTopPos+'px';
            containerDOM.style.height  = (newHeight+10)+'px';
            containerDOM.classList.add(config.cssClasses.scaled);
        }

        function getBreakpoint() {
            var width      = window.innerWidth;
            var breakpoint = '';
            for (var breakpointMinimum in config.responsiveBreakpoints) {
                if (config.responsiveBreakpoints.hasOwnProperty(breakpointMinimum) && width > breakpointMinimum) {
                    breakpoint = config.responsiveBreakpoints[breakpointMinimum];
                }
            }
            return breakpoint;
        }
        function getCookie(name) {
            var dc = document.cookie;
            var prefix = name + "=";
            var begin = dc.indexOf("; " + prefix);
            if (begin == -1) {
                begin = dc.indexOf(prefix);
                if (begin != 0) return null;
            } else {
                begin += 2;
                var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
                if (end == -1) {
                end = dc.length;
                }
            }
            return decodeURI(dc.substring(begin + prefix.length, end));
        }
        function getAuthenticated() {
            if (getCookie('MPP-SessionId') !== null) {
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        }
        function parseConsentCookieValue(cookieValue) {
            var result = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(cookieValue));
            if (typeof result.u !== 'undefined'
            && (result.t !== null && !isNaN(result.t))
            && (result.c === '1' || result.c === '0')) {
                result.c = result.c === '1';
                return result;
            }
            throw new Error('Malformed cookie value');
        }
        function getConsent() {
            var consentCookieValue = getCookie('__rppl_rodo_agrmnt');
            if (consentCookieValue === null) {
                return false;
            } else if (!isNaN(consentCookieValue)) {
                // legacy cookie
                return true;
            } else {
                // most likely proper cookie
                try {
                    var consentData = parseConsentCookieValue(consentCookieValue);
                    return consentData.c;
                } catch (e) {
                    // Invalid cookie format
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        function getTargetString() {
            var loggedIn = getAuthenticated();
            var commercialBrake = false;
            if (getCookie('commercialBrake') !== null) {
                var timestamp = getCookie('commercialBrake');
                var difference = new Date().getTime() - timestamp;
                if(difference <= 60000) {
                    var midnight = new Date();
                    midnight.setHours(24,59,59,1);
                    document.cookie = "commercialBrake="+(timestamp-60000)+";expires="+midnight.toGMTString()+";path=/;domain="+window.location.hostname.match(/.\w*\.\w*$/gi)[0];
                    commercialBrake = true;
                    window.addEventListener('load', () => {
                        document.getElementById('sas_37111_container').classList.remove('ad-labeled');
                    });
                }
            }
            return [
                config.target,
                // 'komponent_'+parentComponents.length,
                'breakpoint-'+getBreakpoint(),
                loggedIn ? 'zalogowany' : 'niezalogowany',
                commercialBrake ? 'commercialBrake' : 'noBrake',
                // getUrlQueryVar('livepreview', document.URL) === 'true' ? 'livepreview' : '',
                getConsent() ? 'consent_1' : 'consent_0'
            ].join(';')
                .split(';')
                .map(function(s) { return s.trim() } )
                .filter(function(s) { return s && s.length > 0})
                .join(';')
                .split(' ')
                .join('_');
        }
        function getUrlQueryVar(name, url) {
            if (!url) url = window.location.href;
            name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, "\\$&");
            var regex = new RegExp("[?&]" + name + "(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)"),
                results = regex.exec(url);
            if (!results) return null;
            if (!results[2]) return '';
            return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, " "));
        }
        function getIds(unique, formatId) {
            if (unique) {
                return {
                    container: 'sas_'+formatId+'_'+unique+'_container',
                    label: 'sas_'+formatId+'_'+unique+'_label',
                    advert: 'sas_'+formatId+'_'+unique
                };
            }
            return {
                container: 'sas_'+formatId+'_container',
                label: 'sas_'+formatId+'_label',
                advert: 'sas_'+formatId
            };
        }
        function getPlacementConfig(opt) {
            var formatName = config.formatsIdToName[opt.formatId];
            var placementConfig = {
                siteId:     opt.sas.siteId,
                pageId:     opt.sas.pageId,
                formats:   opt.formats, // php render all formats
                // formatId:   opt.formatId, // php render all formats
                // formatName: formatName,
                target:     getTargetString()
            };
            if (opt.componentId !== false) {
                placementConfig.tagId = getIds(opt.componentId, opt.formatId).advert
            }
            return placementConfig;
        }
        return {
            getIds: getIds,
            getClasses: function(additional, formatId) {
                return {
                    container: [
                        config.cssClasses.advert,
                        config.cssClasses.formats[formatId],
                        'js-advert-format-'+formatId,
                        config.cssClasses.labeled,
                        config.cssClasses.full,
                        additional
                    ].join(' '),
                    label: config.cssClasses.label
                };
            },
            modify: function(options) {
                var opt = defaultOptions(
                    options,
                    {
                        advertId:   false,
                        scale:      false,
                        height:     false,
                        width:      false,
                        addLabel:   true,
                        addMargins: true,
                        remove:     false
                    }
                );
                var advertDOM    = document.getElementById(opt.advertId)
                var containerDOM = advertDOM.parentNode;
                if (opt.remove) {
                    containerDOM.parentNode.remove(containerDOM);
                    return;
                }
                if (opt.addLabel) {
                    containerDOM.classList.add(config.cssClasses.labeled);
                } else {
                    containerDOM.classList.remove(config.cssClasses.labeled);
                }
                if (opt.addMargins) {
                    containerDOM.classList.add(config.cssClasses.full);
                } else {
                    containerDOM.classList.remove(config.cssClasses.full);
                }
                if (opt.scale) {
                    scale(advertDOM, containerDOM, opt);
                }
            },
            register: function(options) {
                var opt = defaultOptions(
                    options,
                    {
                        formats: false
                    }
                );
                placementConfig  = getPlacementConfig(opt);
                placementOptions = getPlacementOptions();
                sas.cmd.push(function() {
                    sas.call(
                        'onecall',
                        placementConfig,
                        placementOptions
                    );
                });
            },
            render: function(options) {
                var opt = defaultOptions(
                    options,
                    {
                        type: false,
                        sas: false, // defaultOptions injects config if sas equals false
                        formatId: false,
                        lazyLoad: true,
                        formatName: false,
                        componentId: false,
                        breakpoints: false
                    }
                );
                if (!opt.formatId) {
                    return;
                }
                if (opt.sas.disabledFormats.indexOf(opt.formatName) !== -1) {
                    return;
                }
                if (opt.breakpoints && opt.breakpoints.split(',').indexOf(getBreakpoint()) === -1) {
                    var container = document.querySelector('.' + getIds(opt.componentId, opt.formatId).container);
                    container.parentNode.removeChild(container);
                    return;
                }
                if (observer && opt.containerId && opt.lazyLoad && lazyLoadConfig.isPlacementEnabled(opt.formatId)) {
                    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
                        var elementBox = document.getElementById(opt.containerId);
                        observer.observe(elementBox);
                    });
                } else {
                    renderPlacement(opt.formatId + ( opt.type !== 'static' && opt.componentId ? '_'+opt.componentId : ''));
                }
            }
        }
    })(sas, _gremi_adverts, dataLayer, lazyLoadConfiguration);
